<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правдивый.html>правди́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pravdívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>truthfulness, uprightness, veracity
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:правдивость.html>правди́вость</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:изображение.html>изображе́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pravdívostʹ</b> v izobražénii žízni</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">fidelity to life</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***правильность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:правильность.html>пра́вильность</a> (11535)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правильный.html>пра́вильный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právilʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правильность.html>пра́вильность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">právilʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правильность.html>пра́вильности</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>rightness, correctness
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:правильность.html>пра́вильность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:избранный.html>и́збранного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>právilʹnostʹ</b> ízbrannovo putí</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">correctness of the chosen path</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>regularity</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:правильный.html>правильный</a> (2280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правило.html>пра́вило</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právilo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rule</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правильный.html>пра́вильный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">právilʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пра́вильнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пра́вильней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>right, correct</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> regular</li></ol>

***править.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>править</a> (6426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>пра́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">právitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to govern, to rule</li>
<li>to drive, to steer</li>
<li>to correct</li>
<li>to strop, to set</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to edit, i.e. to change the content of a file, a website or the code of software</li></ol>

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>пра́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pravo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Recht</i> and  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">droit</i>, based on <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">right, correct; straight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>пра́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1c  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

***правомерный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:правомерный.html>правоме́рный</a> (30361)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>пра́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мера.html>ме́ра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">méra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">rechtmäßig</i> or  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">gesetzmäßig</i>.
</p>

***правонарушение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:правонарушение.html>правонаруше́ние</a> (20305)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правонарушение.html>правонаруше́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pravonarušénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правонарушение.html>правонаруше́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правонарушение.html>правонаруше́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правонарушение.html>правонаруше́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> violation of the law, offence</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***правопорядок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:правопорядок.html>правопорядок</a> (21874)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правопорядок.html>правопоря́док</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pravoporjádok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правопорядок.html>правопоря́дка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правопорядок.html>правопоря́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правопорядок.html>правопоря́дков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>law and order</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:православие.html>правосла́вие</a> (14956)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀρθοδοξία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">orthodoxía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">correctness in doctrine and belief</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">right, correct</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sláva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glory, glorification; (general) opinion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***правота.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:правота.html>правота́</a> (8418)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правота.html>правота́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pravotá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правота.html>правоты́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>right, rightfulness, correctness
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доказать.html>доказа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:правота.html>правоту́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dokazátʹ svojú <b>pravotú</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prove one's case</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>пра<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1d |   <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> мн. ч. предположительны <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> неупотребимы.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-прав-</b>; суффикс: <b>-от</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

***правый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вый</a> (7369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pravъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ProHwo-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">right judge, master</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*per-</i>. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">právda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prōvincia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">territory, dominion, office, duty, province</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frawjô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lord</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">právyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)праве́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)праве́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>right, right-hand</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> starboard</li>
<li>right-wing</li>
<li>right, correct
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всём</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní <b>právy</b> vo vsjóm.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They <b>are right</b> in everything.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>righteous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>právoje</b> délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">just cause</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In the meaning "correct", the adjective is more commonly used in the short forms. In the meanings "on the right side" and "right-wing", the short forms are rare.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">правору́кий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pravorúkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">právyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вого</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вые</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вых</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вая</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rightist</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:празднество.html>пра́зднество</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prázdnestvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:празднество.html>пра́зднества</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:празднество.html>пра́зднества</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:празднество.html>пра́зднеств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>festival, festivities, celebration</li></ol>

***праздничный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:праздничный.html>пра́здничный</a> (3802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:праздник.html>пра́здник</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prázdnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:праздничный.html>пра́здничный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prázdničnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> holiday
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:праздничный.html>пра́здничный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лагерь.html>ла́герь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prázdničnyj</b> lágerʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>holiday</b> camp</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>festive, festal <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having the atmosphere, decoration, or attitude of a festival, holiday, or celebration</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>пра́зд<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нич<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a.
